**Operating point and voice posture (READ FIRST):** Read `.codex-scratch/review-priority.md` before any other input. It carries the per-repo operating point (stage / user count / cultural emphasis) and the voice-posture rules every finding you produce must follow. Apply `standards.md` § Broken-Glass Test on every finding: questions over prescriptions on every non-bug finding; declarative voice only when you can cite the failing path, the user-observable outcome, and the line where the contract breaks; scope-creep questions must name the cost ("adds complexity and makes PMF iteration harder").

**Q-field shape — REQUIRED on every non-bug question.** Every question (in Open Questions, in REFRAME-AS-QUESTION reframes, in scope-creep prompts) MUST be about external state — user behavior, data shape, OS contract, deadline, scale, production observation. NEVER about whether to apply the proposed code change.

The test: replace the question with "Will [premise] hold in the world?" — does that read as a fact you could in principle verify by looking at user data, an OS manual, or production logs? If yes, the Q is well-formed. If the only way to "verify" the Q is to make the code change and see, the Q is begging the question and must be rewritten.

Wrong-shape examples (these fail review):
- ✗ "Does the lifecycle ever fire?" — about code paths; circular
- ✗ "Can the parser live in one helper?" — about the proposed solution
- ✗ "Will we maintain X as one contract?" — begs the question
- ✗ "Should we extract this into a helper?" — asks about the action

Right-shape examples (each Q is about an external fact whose answer dictates whether the proposed action is worth the cost):
- ✓ "Will hdiutil's output format drift across macOS versions?" — answer dictates whether the helper extraction pays for itself
- ✓ "Do users ever have negative bank balances?" — checkable via prod data
- ✓ "Will the connector list grow past 8 entries before PMF?" — checkable via roadmap
- ✓ "Will errors here be observed in production at our current call volume?" — checkable via logs

**Broken-Glass is pro-simplification.** Broken-Glass Test means *push for elegant code that lets the team validate the product faster*. DRY refactors, removing duplication, collapsing branches, deleting dead code — these are aligned WITH the rule, not against it. The push-back the rule provides applies to *adding* architecture for hypothetical scale, not to *removing* duplication that already exists.

NEVER cite Broken-Glass Test as a reason to decline a simplification finding. If a finding asks to remove code (DRY, dead code, unreachable branch), the default is to apply it; the burden shifts to naming why keeping the existing complexity is worth it.

Wrong-application example (this is the failure mode that motivated this rule):
- ✗ "Broken-Glass Test: this is a code-quality question, not a failing-path bug — keep the duplicate parser code as-is."

Right-application example:
- ✓ "DRY this — Broken-Glass favors collapsing the 3-place parser into one helper. Severity stays low (it's tech debt, not a failing bug), but the recommendation is to simplify, not to decline simplification."

This is how you separate "author misunderstood an invariant" from "author is changing a documented behavior on purpose."

1. Read `.codex-scratch/diff.patch` first. Then open the touched files themselves and read enough of them to understand context — call sites, definitions, invariants. Do NOT skim the diff and produce a verdict; a good specialist traces how the changes interact with the rest of the codebase.
2. Focus ONLY on your specialist angle (specified below). Do not duplicate other angles.
3. Output in this exact shape:

```
## [performance] findings

<one paragraph — what is wrong, why it matters, where>
Files: path/to/file.ext:LINE (and additional citations as needed)

### Finding 2 — <severity>

```

4. Severity is exactly one of: `blocking`, `medium`, `low`, `nit`. Use `blocking` ONLY for issues that must be fixed before merge.
5. The Surveyed section is REQUIRED even if you have zero findings. A specialist that returns only "No findings" has failed to do its job. If after surveying you genuinely have nothing to raise, output the Surveyed section alone, with each bullet marked `clean` and a brief reason.
6. Be specific. Cite file paths and line numbers. Quote the problematic code in ≤2 lines when it clarifies. **Name the user impact when there is one** — "users retrying a failed payment can be charged twice" beats "this is a race condition." If a finding is purely internal (tech debt, refactoring, DRY), skip the user-impact framing rather than invent one.
7. Keep each finding under 120 words. No preamble, no conclusion, no verdict. The aggregator will assemble the final review.
8. **Remedy-cost framing.** When you raise a finding, name the cost of the remedy you'd propose, not just the LOC delta. The cost is **conditionals + special cases + defensive branches + new abstractions** — LOC is a stand-in for those. The user's standards weight engineer time over compute time, so a remedy that adds N branches for a scenario that doesn't happen is bloat regardless of how the line count nets out. **Don't propose:** defensive guards on internal callers, fallback chains for hypothetical state pollution, type validation outside trust boundaries, wrapper dataclasses for one call site, streaming/incremental rewrites of small in-memory operations on theoretical perf grounds, or extra error handling on fail-fast paths. The test for any edge-case handler: *does the edge case actually happen, or will it in the near future?* If neither, drop the remedy and (depending on whether the underlying finding still stands) downgrade severity or omit the finding. Cite `Concise Code` and `Fail-Fast` from the standards when you flag this in your own output.

**Your angle: Performance and scale — bias toward concise/elegant fixes only.**

FIRST, read `.codex-scratch/standards.md` § Concise Code and § Fail-Fast. Your bias is anti-premature-optimization. Engineer-hours are the cost we minimize, not CPU. Simple infra wins (sqlite + readable ORM > distributed caches + hand-rolled queries).

ALSO read: `.codex-scratch/inferred-intent.md`, `.codex-scratch/diff.patch`, `.codex-scratch/product-context.md`.

**The failure mode you exist to catch:** code that ships, passes CI, then OOMs / times out / falls over in prod under realistic load — *with a fix that is small and idiomatic*. You are NOT here to find "could be faster" cases that need new infra or restructuring. You are here to catch real bugs whose fix is a one-liner the author would have written if they'd thought of it.

**Method (walk the diff for unhappy edges, like data-integrity but for cost):**

For each new code path, ask:
- Will this run for every request, per-N-records, or per-user? Multiply by current scale.
- Is there a loop with a DB / HTTP / file call inside that should be batched?
- Is there a SELECT / fetch without a LIMIT or pagination on data that grows with users?
- Is there sync I/O on an async path? (Blocks the event loop — one slow request stalls everything.)
- Is there `O(n²)` work where `n` is user-controlled and growing?
- Is `.count()` or `.all()` used where `.exists()` or `.filter().exists()` would do?
- Is invariant work (regex compile, dict construction, lookup) inside a loop body?

**Common bug classes — and the canonical fix shape:**

| Bug class | Example | Fix shape |
|---|---|---|
| N+1 ORM | `for user in users: user.posts.count()` | `select_related` / `prefetch_related` / batched fetch |
| Unbounded fetch | `Model.objects.all()` returned to a handler | `LIMIT` + pagination, or `.iterator()` |
| Sync-in-async | `requests.get(...)` inside an `async def` | `httpx.AsyncClient` or move to a worker |
| Count-instead-of-exists | `if Q.count() > 0:` | `if Q.exists():` |
| Re-compile in loop | `re.compile(...)` inside a loop | hoist to module level |
| Load-to-count | `len(list(qs))` | `qs.count()` |
| O(n²) membership | `for x in a: if x in b:` where `b` is a list | `set(b)` once |

**Severity:**
- `blocking` — *either* (a) this WILL OOM / time out / crash at current or known-near-term scale, *OR* (b) the fix is one-line idiomatic AND the bug is real (not theoretical). Either condition is independently sufficient.
- `medium` — real perf concern with a clear simple fix, no crash imminent.
- `low` — observation worth noting; fix would add complexity.
- Don't pad with "no findings." The Surveyed section is where you prove you looked.

**Disallowed findings (DO NOT FILE):**

- "Add Redis / memcached / a caching layer." — adds infra.
- "Switch from sqlite / Postgres to <X>." — infrastructure decision.
- "Hand-roll this ORM query as raw SQL for X% speedup." — degrades readability for real cost.
- "Denormalize the schema." — cross-cutting redesign.
- "Add a CDN / queue / worker pool." — infra.
- "Split this into a microservice." — architecture, not perf.
- "Use Cython / Rust / a faster language." — out of scope.

The bar: if the fix grows infra, adds dependencies, or trades readability for throughput, the finding is out of scope here. **Engineer-hours, not CPU.** A 2× speedup that costs a week of engineer time and adds a moving part is a *bad* finding for this team's stage.

Where this overlaps with other specialists:
- `data-integrity` walks unhappy edges for correctness; you walk them for cost.
- `simplification` may catch a verbose pattern that's also slow — let them own DRY/concision; you own the perf framing.

Out of scope: correctness bugs, security, test coverage, architecture fit.

Look beyond the diff: grep how the touched function is invoked across the repo. The same code is `blocking`-perf in a request handler and `low`-perf in a daily report job.

+#!/usr/bin/env bash
+# Mount a Plow DMG and assert it has no custom volume icon (PLO-29 regression
+# guard) and that the volume name is "Plow". Detaches before exiting.
+set -euo pipefail
+
+usage() {
+  cat <<'EOF'
+Usage: plowd-verify-dmg [--dmg <path>]
+
+Mounts the given DMG, asserts the mounted volume is named "Plow" and has no
+.VolumeIcon.icns at its root, then detaches. Defaults to .build/Plow.dmg
+relative to the repo root.
+EOF
+}
+
+repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"
+dmg_path="${repo_root}/.build/Plow.dmg"
+
+while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
+  case "$1" in
+    --dmg)
+      dmg_path="${2:-}"
+      shift 2
+      ;;
+    -h|--help)
+      usage
+      exit 0
+      ;;
+    *)
+      echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
+      usage >&2
+      exit 1
+      ;;
+  esac
+done
+
+if [[ "${dmg_path}" != /* ]]; then
+  dmg_path="${repo_root}/${dmg_path}"
+fi
+
+[[ -f "${dmg_path}" ]] || { echo "error: DMG not found: ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+# Refuse to run when a Plow volume is already mounted: the new mountpoint
+# would be "Plow 1" / "Plow 2" / ..., which would mask a real regression in
+# the volume-name assertion below.
+mounted_plow_volumes="$(hdiutil info 2>/dev/null | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true)"
+mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"
+if [[ -n "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]]; then
+  echo "error: a Plow volume is already mounted; eject it before verifying:" >&2
+  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
+  exit 1
+fi
+
+mounted_volume=""
+cleanup() {
+  local rc=$?
+  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
+    if [[ "${rc}" -eq 0 ]]; then
+      # Success path: detach failure (e.g. volume busy) must be fatal.
+      # Otherwise the next release retry trips ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume
+      # in plowd-beta-package-signed and aborts on a leaked mount.
+      if ! hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}"; then
+        echo "error: failed to detach ${mounted_volume} after successful verify" >&2
+        exit 1
+      fi
+    else
+      # Failure path: don't let detach noise mask the real error.
+      hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
+    fi
+  fi
+  exit "${rc}"
+}
+trap cleanup EXIT
+
+attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${dmg_path}" -nobrowse -readonly)"
+mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | sed -n 's|.*\(/Volumes/.*\)$|\1|p' | head -n 1)"
+[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to mount ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+volume_name="$(basename "${mounted_volume}")"
+[[ "${volume_name}" == "Plow" ]] || { echo "error: mounted volume name is '${volume_name}', expected 'Plow'" >&2; exit 1; }
+
+[[ ! -e "${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns" ]] || {
+  echo "error: ${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns exists; PLO-29 regression: DMG ships a custom volume icon" >&2
+  exit 1
+}
+
+echo "ok: ${dmg_path} mounts as 'Plow' with no custom volume icon"

+@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
+def test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_dmg_shipping_volume_icon(tmp_path):
+    """PLO-29 artifact-level guard. Catches the failure mode that
+    ``test_signed_package_script_builds_ulfo_dmg_without_staging_ds_store``
+    cannot: a regression that re-attaches the DMG post-``hdiutil create``
+    and re-stages a custom volume icon at the final-image stage. We build
+    three real DMGs with hdiutil and assert plowd-verify-dmg accepts the
+    clean one and rejects each regression shape.
+
+    plowd-verify-dmg is wired into plowd-beta-package-signed between staple
+    and S3 upload, so a rejection here aborts ``just release`` before any
+    artifact ships."""
+    # Refuse to run if a real Plow volume is already mounted: the script
+    # bails on that and our assertions would tag the wrong failure mode.
+    info = subprocess.run(
+        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
+    )
+    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
+        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
+
+    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
+    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
+    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
+
+    def make_dmg(dmg_path: Path, *, volname: str) -> None:
+        subprocess.run(
+            [
+                "hdiutil", "create",
+                "-volname", volname,
+                "-srcfolder", str(stage),
+                "-ov",
+                "-format", "ULFO",
+                str(dmg_path),
+            ],
+            check=True, capture_output=True,
+        )
+
+    def run_verify(dmg_path: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
+        return subprocess.run(
+            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), "--dmg", str(dmg_path)],
+            capture_output=True, text=True,
+        )
+
+    # Happy path: clean Plow DMG with no .VolumeIcon must pass.
+    clean_dmg = tmp_path / "clean.dmg"
+    make_dmg(clean_dmg, volname="Plow")
+    ok = run_verify(clean_dmg)
+    assert ok.returncode == 0, f"clean DMG rejected: stdout={ok.stdout!r} stderr={ok.stderr!r}"
+
+    # Regression #1: someone re-introduces .VolumeIcon.icns at the volume root.
+    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").write_text("fake-icns")
+    iconed_dmg = tmp_path / "iconed.dmg"
+    make_dmg(iconed_dmg, volname="Plow")
+    fail = run_verify(iconed_dmg)
+    assert fail.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG that ships .VolumeIcon.icns"
+    assert ".VolumeIcon.icns exists" in fail.stderr
+
+    # Regression #2: someone parameterizes -volname to something other than "Plow".
+    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").unlink()
+    misnamed_dmg = tmp_path / "misnamed.dmg"
+    make_dmg(misnamed_dmg, volname="NotPlow")
+    fail2 = run_verify(misnamed_dmg)
+    assert fail2.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG with wrong volume name"
+    assert "expected 'Plow'" in fail2.stderr
+
+
+@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
+def test_plowd_verify_dmg_propagates_detach_failure_on_success_path(tmp_path):
+    """Round-2: if `hdiutil detach` fails on the success path (e.g. the
+    volume is busy), plowd-verify-dmg must exit non-zero. The previous
+    `|| true` swallowed the failure and returned 0, leaking /Volumes/Plow,
+    which then tripped ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume on the next release
+    retry. This test injects an `hdiutil` wrapper whose `detach` always
+    fails and asserts the script surfaces it."""
+    info = subprocess.run(
+        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
+    )
+    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
+        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
+
+    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
+    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
+    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
+    dmg = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
+    subprocess.run(
+        [
+            "hdiutil", "create",
+            "-volname", "Plow",
+            "-srcfolder", str(stage),
+            "-ov",
+            "-format", "ULFO",
+            str(dmg),
+        ],
+        check=True, capture_output=True,
+    )
+
+    real_hdiutil = subprocess.run(
+        ["which", "hdiutil"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
+    ).stdout.strip()
+    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
+    fake_bin.mkdir()
+    wrapper = fake_bin / "hdiutil"
+    wrapper.write_text(
+        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\n"
+        f'if [[ "$1" == "detach" ]]; then\n'
+        f'  echo "fake: detach failure (test injection)" >&2\n'
+        f'  exit 16\n'
+        f'fi\n'
+        f'exec "{real_hdiutil}" "$@"\n'
+    )
+    wrapper.chmod(0o755)
+
+    try:
+        result = subprocess.run(
+            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), "--dmg", str(dmg)],
+            capture_output=True, text=True,
+            env={
+                **subprocess.os.environ,
+                "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
+            },
+        )
+        assert result.returncode != 0, (
+            f"verify-dmg returned 0 despite detach failure; mount leaked.\n"
+            f"stdout={result.stdout!r}\nstderr={result.stderr!r}"
+        )
+        assert "failed to detach" in result.stderr, (
+            f"expected 'failed to detach' in stderr, got: {result.stderr!r}"
+        )
+    finally:
+        # Real hdiutil to clean up the leaked mount the wrapper refused to release.
+        subprocess.run(
+            [real_hdiutil, "detach", "/Volumes/Plow"],
+            capture_output=True,
+        )
+
+

     output = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"

     2	# Mount a Plow DMG and assert it has no custom volume icon (PLO-29 regression
     3	# guard) and that the volume name is "Plow". Detaches before exiting.

     8	Usage: plowd-verify-dmg [--dmg <path>]
     9	
    10	Mounts the given DMG, asserts the mounted volume is named "Plow" and has no
    11	.VolumeIcon.icns at its root, then detaches. Defaults to .build/Plow.dmg
    12	relative to the repo root.
    13	EOF
    14	}

    42	
    43	# Refuse to run when a Plow volume is already mounted: the new mountpoint
    44	# would be "Plow 1" / "Plow 2" / ..., which would mask a real regression in
    45	# the volume-name assertion below.
    46	mounted_plow_volumes="$(hdiutil info 2>/dev/null | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true)"
    47	mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"

    51	  exit 1

    55	cleanup() {
    56	  local rc=$?
    57	  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
    58	    if [[ "${rc}" -eq 0 ]]; then
    59	      # Success path: detach failure (e.g. volume busy) must be fatal.
    60	      # Otherwise the next release retry trips ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume
    61	      # in plowd-beta-package-signed and aborts on a leaked mount.
    62	      if ! hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}"; then
    63	        echo "error: failed to detach ${mounted_volume} after successful verify" >&2
    64	        exit 1
    65	      fi
    66	    else
    67	      # Failure path: don't let detach noise mask the real error.
    68	      hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
    69	    fi
    70	  fi
    71	  exit "${rc}"
    72	}
    73	trap cleanup EXIT
    74

    76	mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | sed -n 's|.*\(/Volumes/.*\)$|\1|p' | head -n 1)"

    78	
    79	volume_name="$(basename "${mounted_volume}")"

    84	  exit 1
    85	}

   155	fi
   156	[[ -d "${app_bundle}" ]] || { echo "error: app bundle not found: ${app_bundle}" >&2; exit 1; }
   157	[[ -f "${entitlements}" ]] || { echo "error: entitlements file not found: ${entitlements}" >&2; exit 1; }
   158	[[ -f "${limactl_entitlements}" ]] || { echo "error: limactl entitlements file not found: ${limactl_entitlements}" >&2; exit 1; }
   159	[[ -x "${validate_script}" ]] || { echo "error: package validator not found: ${validate_script}" >&2; exit 1; }
   160	[[ -x "${stage_sparkle_script}" ]] || { echo "error: Sparkle stage script not found: ${stage_sparkle_script}" >&2; exit 1; }
   161	[[ -x "${publish_sparkle_script}" ]] || { echo "error: Sparkle publish script not found: ${publish_sparkle_script}" >&2; exit 1; }
   162	[[ -f "${dmg_background}" ]] || { echo "error: DMG background not found: ${dmg_background}" >&2; exit 1; }
   163	
   164	echo "validating packaged app bundle..."
   165	"${validate_script}" --app-bundle "${app_bundle}"
   166	
   167	version="$(plist_read "${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" CFBundleShortVersionString)"
   168	build_number="$(plist_read "${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" CFBundleVersion)"
   169	sparkle_feed_url="$(plist_read "${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" SUFeedURL)"
   170	sparkle_public_key="$(plist_read "${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" SUPublicEDKey)"
   171	
   172	[[ -n "${version}" ]] || { echo "error: missing CFBundleShortVersionString in ${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" >&2; exit 1; }
   173	[[ -n "${build_number}" ]] || { echo "error: missing CFBundleVersion in ${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" >&2; exit 1; }
   174	[[ -n "${sparkle_feed_url}" ]] || { echo "error: missing SUFeedURL in ${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" >&2; exit 1; }
   175	[[ -n "${sparkle_public_key}" ]] || { echo "error: missing SUPublicEDKey in ${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" >&2; exit 1; }
   176	
   177	release_prefix="${release_prefix#/}"
   178	release_prefix="${release_prefix%/}"
   179	prefix_with_slash=""
   180	if [[ -n "${release_prefix}" ]]; then
   181	  prefix_with_slash="${release_prefix}/"
   182	fi
   183	dmg_key="${prefix_with_slash}downloads/Plow-${version}-${build_number}.dmg"
   184	dmg_sha_key="${dmg_key}.sha256"

   190	echo "preferred Apple team id: ${team_id}"
   191	echo "using notary profile: ${notary_profile}"
   192	
   193	for cmd in aws codesign ditto file find hdiutil shasum xattr xcrun; do
   194	  command -v "${cmd}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || { echo "error: required command not found: ${cmd}" >&2; exit 1; }
   195	done

   197	ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume
   198	
   199	stage_dir="$(mktemp -d /tmp/phoenix-signed-beta.XXXXXX)"
   200	stage_app="${stage_dir}/Plow.app"
   201	sparkle_stage_dir="$(mktemp -d /tmp/phoenix-sparkle-feed.XXXXXX)"
   202	mounted_volume=""
   203	
   204	cleanup() {
   205	  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
   206	    hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
   207	  fi
   208	  rm -rf "${stage_dir}"
   209	  rm -rf "${sparkle_stage_dir}"
   210	}
   211	trap cleanup EXIT
   212	
   213	mkdir -p "$(dirname "${output}")"
   214	ditto "${app_bundle}" "${stage_app}"
   215	mkdir -p "${stage_dir}/.background"
   216	ditto "${dmg_background}" "${stage_dir}/.background/background.tiff"
   217	ln -s /Applications "${stage_dir}/Applications"
   218	xattr -cr "${stage_app}"
   219	
   220	while IFS= read -r -d '' file_path; do
   221	  file_desc="$(file -b "${file_path}" 2>/dev/null || true)"
   222	  if [[ "${file_desc}" == *"Mach-O"* ]]; then
   223	    sign_args=(--force --sign "${identity}" --timestamp)
   224	    if [[ "${file_desc}" == *"executable"* ]]; then
   225	      sign_args+=(--options runtime)
   226	    fi
   227	    if [[ "${file_path}" == "${stage_app}/Contents/Resources/bin/limactl" ]]; then
   228	      sign_args+=(--entitlements "${limactl_entitlements}")
   229	    fi
   230	    codesign "${sign_args[@]}" "${file_path}"
   231	  fi
   232	done < <(find "${stage_app}" -type f -print0)
   233	
   234	codesign \
   235	  --force \
   236	  --sign "${identity}" \
   237	  --timestamp \
   238	  --options runtime \
   239	  --entitlements "${entitlements}" \
   240	  "${stage_app}"
   241	
   242	codesign --verify --deep --strict --verbose=4 "${stage_app}"
   243	
   244	if [[ "${keep_signed_app}" == "1" ]]; then
   245	  preserved_app="${repo_root}/.build/Plow-signed.app"
   246	  rm -rf "${preserved_app}"
   247	  ditto "${stage_app}" "${preserved_app}"
   248	  codesign --verify --deep --strict --verbose=4 "${preserved_app}"
   249	  echo "preserved signed app for inspection: ${preserved_app}"
   250	fi
   251	
   252	"${stage_sparkle_script}" \
   253	  --app-bundle "${stage_app}" \
   254	  --archives-dir "${sparkle_stage_dir}" \
   255	  --download-url-prefix "${sparkle_download_url_prefix}" \
   256	  --account "${sparkle_account}"
   257	
   258	rm -f "${output}" "${output}.sha256"
   259	echo "creating DMG..."
   260	hdiutil create \
   261	  -volname "Plow" \
   262	  -srcfolder "${stage_dir}" \
   263	  -ov \
   264	  -format ULFO \
   265	  "${output}"
   266	
   267	echo "verifying mounted app from DMG..."
   268	attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${output}" -nobrowse)"
   269	mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | sed -n 's|.*\(/Volumes/.*\)$|\1|p' | head -n 1)"
   270	[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to determine mounted volume for ${output}" >&2; exit 1; }
   271	codesign --verify --deep --strict --verbose=4 "${mounted_volume}/Plow.app"
   272	hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null
   273	mounted_volume=""
   274	
   275	echo "submitting DMG to Apple notarization..."
   276	submit_output="$(xcrun notarytool submit "${output}" --keychain-profile "${notary_profile}" --wait --output-format json)"
   277	submit_id="$(python3 -c 'import json,sys; print(json.load(sys.stdin).get("id",""))' <<<"${submit_output}")"
   278	submit_status="$(python3 -c 'import json,sys; print(json.load(sys.stdin).get("status",""))' <<<"${submit_output}")"
   279	if [[ "${submit_status}" != "Accepted" ]]; then
   280	  echo "notarization failed with status: ${submit_status:-unknown}" >&2
   281	  if [[ -n "${submit_id}" ]]; then
   282	    echo "submission id: ${submit_id}" >&2
   283	    xcrun notarytool log "${submit_id}" --keychain-profile "${notary_profile}" || true
   284	  fi
   285	  exit 1
   286	fi
   287	echo "stapling notarization ticket..."
   288	xcrun stapler staple "${output}"
   289	echo "checking local Gatekeeper assessment for the DMG..."
   290	if ! spctl --assess --type open -vv "${output}"; then
   291	  echo "warning: local spctl assessment of the DMG failed; notarization was accepted and the ticket was stapled" >&2
   292	fi
   293	
   294	# PLO-29: verify the final shipping artifact has no custom volume icon and
   295	# that the volume name is "Plow" before it gets uploaded. plowd-verify-dmg
   296	# performs a real `hdiutil attach` of the stapled DMG, so this can only run
   297	# against a real filesystem; the unit-test path that stubs hdiutil sets
   298	# PLOW_SKIP_DMG_VERIFY=1.
   299	if [[ "${PLOW_SKIP_DMG_VERIFY:-0}" != "1" ]]; then
   300	  echo "verifying final DMG against PLO-29 contract..."
   301	  "${repo_root}/app/plowd/scripts/plowd-verify-dmg" --dmg "${output}"
   302	fi
   303	
   304	echo "writing checksum..."
   305	shasum -a 256 "${output}" > "${output}.sha256"
   306	
   307	echo "signed distribution image created: ${output}"
   308	echo "sha256 file: ${output}.sha256"
   309	profile_args=()
   310	if [[ -n "${s3_profile}" ]]; then
   311	  profile_args=(--profile "${s3_profile}")
   312	fi
   313	
   314	echo "uploading versioned DMG artifacts to S3..."
   315	aws s3 cp "${output}" "s3://${s3_bucket}/${dmg_key}" ${profile_args[@]+"${profile_args[@]}"}
   316	aws s3 cp "${output}.sha256" "s3://${s3_bucket}/${dmg_sha_key}" ${profile_args[@]+"${profile_args[@]}"}

   321	  --s3-bucket "${s3_bucket}"
   322	  --appcast-key "${sparkle_appcast_key}"
   323	  --archive-prefix "${sparkle_archive_prefix}"

   330	echo "  Appcast: https://s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/${s3_bucket}/${sparkle_appcast_key}"

    20	def _provision_fake_bin(fake_bin: Path, systemctl_log: Path) -> None:
    21	    """Write stub commands sufficient to run provision-runtime.sh on macOS."""
    22	    stubs = {
    23	        # zstd just needs to be on PATH so the apt-get install branch is skipped
    24	        "zstd": "#!/bin/sh\n",
    25	        # sha256sum: hash stdin or file args, mimicking GNU coreutils behaviour
    26	        "sha256sum": textwrap.dedent("""\
    27	            #!/usr/bin/env python3
    28	            import hashlib, sys
    29	            from pathlib import Path
    30	            args = [a for a in sys.argv[1:] if a != "--"]
    31	            if args:
    32	                for arg in args:
    33	                    try:
    34	                        data = Path(arg).read_bytes()
    35	                        print(hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest() + "  " + arg)
    36	                    except FileNotFoundError:
    37	                        print(f"sha256sum: {arg}: No such file or directory", file=sys.stderr)
    38	                        sys.exit(1)
    39	            else:
    40	                data = sys.stdin.buffer.read()
    41	                print(hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest() + "  -")
    42	            """),
    43	        # systemctl: log every invocation; always succeed
    44	        "systemctl": f'#!/bin/sh\necho "$@" >> "{systemctl_log}"\n',
    45	    }
    46	    for name, body in stubs.items():
    47	        p = fake_bin / name
    48	        p.write_text(body)
    49	        p.chmod(0o755)
    50

    52	def _run_provision(tmp_path: Path, fake_bin: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
    53	    unit_dir = tmp_path / "units"
    54	    unit_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    55	    libexec_dir = tmp_path / "libexec"
    56	    libexec_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    57	    return subprocess.run(
    58	        ["bash", str(PROVISION_SCRIPT)],
    59	        capture_output=True,
    60	        text=True,
    61	        env={
    62	            **subprocess.os.environ,
    63	            "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
    64	            "PLOW_UNIT_DIR": str(unit_dir),
    65	            "PLOW_LIBEXEC_DIR": str(libexec_dir),
    66	        },
    67	    )

    70	def test_provision_restarts_containerd_on_first_run(tmp_path):
    71	    """containerd.service is restarted when unit files are written for the first time."""
    72	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
    73	    fake_bin.mkdir()
    74	    systemctl_log = tmp_path / "systemctl.log"
    75	    _provision_fake_bin(fake_bin, systemctl_log)
    76	
    77	    result = _run_provision(tmp_path, fake_bin)
    78	    assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
    79	
    80	    calls = systemctl_log.read_text().splitlines()
    81	    assert any("restart containerd.service" in c for c in calls)

    84	def test_provision_skips_containerd_restart_when_units_unchanged(tmp_path):
    85	    """containerd.service is not restarted when provision writes identical unit files."""
    86	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
    87	    fake_bin.mkdir()
    88	    systemctl_log = tmp_path / "systemctl.log"
    89	    _provision_fake_bin(fake_bin, systemctl_log)
    90	
    91	    # First run — creates units from scratch; restart expected
    92	    r1 = _run_provision(tmp_path, fake_bin)
    93	    assert r1.returncode == 0, r1.stderr
    94	
    95	    # Second run — same unit content; containerd restart must be skipped
    96	    systemctl_log.unlink()
    97	    r2 = _run_provision(tmp_path, fake_bin)
    98	    assert r2.returncode == 0, r2.stderr
    99	
   100	    calls = systemctl_log.read_text().splitlines() if systemctl_log.exists() else []
   101	    assert not any("restart containerd.service" in c for c in calls), (
   102	        f"containerd was restarted on unchanged provision run:\n" + "\n".join(calls)
   103	    )

   254	@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
   255	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_dmg_shipping_volume_icon(tmp_path):
   256	    """PLO-29 artifact-level guard. Catches the failure mode that
   257	    ``test_signed_package_script_builds_ulfo_dmg_without_staging_ds_store``
   258	    cannot: a regression that re-attaches the DMG post-``hdiutil create``
   259	    and re-stages a custom volume icon at the final-image stage. We build
   260	    three real DMGs with hdiutil and assert plowd-verify-dmg accepts the
   261	    clean one and rejects each regression shape.
   262	
   263	    plowd-verify-dmg is wired into plowd-beta-package-signed between staple
   264	    and S3 upload, so a rejection here aborts ``just release`` before any
   265	    artifact ships."""
   266	    # Refuse to run if a real Plow volume is already mounted: the script
   267	    # bails on that and our assertions would tag the wrong failure mode.
   268	    info = subprocess.run(
   269	        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   270	    )
   271	    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
   272	        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
   273	
   274	    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
   275	    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
   276	    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
   277	
   278	    def make_dmg(dmg_path: Path, *, volname: str) -> None:
   279	        subprocess.run(
   280	            [
   281	                "hdiutil", "create",
   282	                "-volname", volname,
   283	                "-srcfolder", str(stage),
   284	                "-ov",
   285	                "-format", "ULFO",
   286	                str(dmg_path),
   287	            ],
   288	            check=True, capture_output=True,
   289	        )
   290	
   291	    def run_verify(dmg_path: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
   292	        return subprocess.run(
   293	            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), "--dmg", str(dmg_path)],
   294	            capture_output=True, text=True,
   295	        )
   296	
   297	    # Happy path: clean Plow DMG with no .VolumeIcon must pass.
   298	    clean_dmg = tmp_path / "clean.dmg"
   299	    make_dmg(clean_dmg, volname="Plow")
   300	    ok = run_verify(clean_dmg)
   301	    assert ok.returncode == 0, f"clean DMG rejected: stdout={ok.stdout!r} stderr={ok.stderr!r}"
   302	
   303	    # Regression #1: someone re-introduces .VolumeIcon.icns at the volume root.
   304	    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").write_text("fake-icns")
   305	    iconed_dmg = tmp_path / "iconed.dmg"
   306	    make_dmg(iconed_dmg, volname="Plow")
   307	    fail = run_verify(iconed_dmg)
   308	    assert fail.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG that ships .VolumeIcon.icns"
   309	    assert ".VolumeIcon.icns exists" in fail.stderr
   310	
   311	    # Regression #2: someone parameterizes -volname to something other than "Plow".
   312	    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").unlink()
   313	    misnamed_dmg = tmp_path / "misnamed.dmg"
   314	    make_dmg(misnamed_dmg, volname="NotPlow")
   315	    fail2 = run_verify(misnamed_dmg)
   316	    assert fail2.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG with wrong volume name"
   317	    assert "expected 'Plow'" in fail2.stderr
   318	
   319	
   320	@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
   321	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_propagates_detach_failure_on_success_path(tmp_path):
   322	    """Round-2: if `hdiutil detach` fails on the success path (e.g. the
   323	    volume is busy), plowd-verify-dmg must exit non-zero. The previous
   324	    `|| true` swallowed the failure and returned 0, leaking /Volumes/Plow,
   325	    which then tripped ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume on the next release
   326	    retry. This test injects an `hdiutil` wrapper whose `detach` always
   327	    fails and asserts the script surfaces it."""
   328	    info = subprocess.run(
   329	        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   330	    )
   331	    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
   332	        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
   333	
   334	    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
   335	    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
   336	    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
   337	    dmg = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
   338	    subprocess.run(
   339	        [
   340	            "hdiutil", "create",
   341	            "-volname", "Plow",
   342	            "-srcfolder", str(stage),
   343	            "-ov",
   344	            "-format", "ULFO",
   345	            str(dmg),
   346	        ],
   347	        check=True, capture_output=True,
   348	    )
   349	
   350	    real_hdiutil = subprocess.run(
   351	        ["which", "hdiutil"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   352	    ).stdout.strip()
   353	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
   354	    fake_bin.mkdir()
   355	    wrapper = fake_bin / "hdiutil"
   356	    wrapper.write_text(
   357	        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\n"
   358	        f'if [[ "$1" == "detach" ]]; then\n'
   359	        f'  echo "fake: detach failure (test injection)" >&2\n'
   360	        f'  exit 16\n'
   361	        f'fi\n'
   362	        f'exec "{real_hdiutil}" "$@"\n'
   363	    )
   364	    wrapper.chmod(0o755)
   365	
   366	    try:
   367	        result = subprocess.run(
   368	            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), "--dmg", str(dmg)],
   369	            capture_output=True, text=True,
   370	            env={
   371	                **subprocess.os.environ,
   372	                "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
   373	            },
   374	        )
   375	        assert result.returncode != 0, (
   376	            f"verify-dmg returned 0 despite detach failure; mount leaked.\n"
   377	            f"stdout={result.stdout!r}\nstderr={result.stderr!r}"
   378	        )
   379	        assert "failed to detach" in result.stderr, (
   380	            f"expected 'failed to detach' in stderr, got: {result.stderr!r}"
   381	        )
   382	    finally:
   383	        # Real hdiutil to clean up the leaked mount the wrapper refused to release.
   384	        subprocess.run(
   385	            [real_hdiutil, "detach", "/Volumes/Plow"],
   386	            capture_output=True,
   387	        )
   388

From 4edb57969ae7e2863b328ba5055e5ce1511e9974 Mon Sep 17 00:00:00 2001
From: Swagat Patel <swagatpatel@users.noreply.github.com>
Date: Thu, 30 Apr 2026 18:20:56 -0700
Subject: [PATCH 1/9] PLO-29: drop custom DMG volume icon
MIME-Version: 1.0
Content-Type: text/plain; charset=UTF-8
Content-Transfer-Encoding: 8bit

Mounted Plow DMGs were showing the app icon, which Sam reported as
indistinguishable from the running app in Finder. Strip the custom
icon so the mounted volume uses the default macOS removable-volume
icon while keeping the volume name "Plow".

- plowd-beta-package-signed: stop staging .VolumeIcon.icns; create the
  ULFO DMG directly instead of going UDRW -> attach -> set
  kHasCustomIcon FinderInfo -> detach -> convert. The dance only
  existed to host the icon flag.
- delete the now-orphaned app/plowd/dmg/volume.icns asset.
- add plowd-verify-dmg + `just app dmg-verify` recipe: mounts a built
  DMG, asserts the volume name is "Plow" and that no .VolumeIcon.icns
  ships at the volume root. Smoke-tested locally on three paths
  (happy / .VolumeIcon present / wrong volname) — all behave.
- test_signed_package_script_builds_ulfo_dmg_without_staging_ds_store:
  pin the new contract (no .VolumeIcon.icns staged, no UDRW/convert).

Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.7 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>

     1	#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2	# Build, sign, notarize, staple, and upload a Plow DMG.
     3	set -euo pipefail
     4	
     5	usage() {
     6	  cat <<'EOF'
     7	Usage: plowd-beta-package-signed [options]
     8	
     9	Options:
    10	  --app-bundle <path>       Built Plow.app bundle to package
    11	  --output <path>           Output DMG path
    12	  --entitlements <path>     Entitlements plist for the top-level app signature
    13	  --identity <value>        Developer ID Application signing identity
    14	  --notary-profile <name>   notarytool keychain profile name
    15	  --s3-bucket <name>        S3 bucket for upload
    16	  --release-prefix <path>   Optional S3 prefix for versioned release artifacts
    17	  --s3-profile <name>       AWS profile name
    18	  --sparkle-account <name>  Sparkle keychain account name for generate_appcast
    19	  -h, --help                Show this help
    20	
    21	Environment:
    22	  PLOW_CODESIGN_IDENTITY    Default signing identity if --identity is omitted
    23	  PLOW_APPLE_TEAM_ID        Apple team id for identity auto-detection
    24	  PLOW_NOTARY_PROFILE       Default notary profile if --notary-profile is omitted
    25	  PLOW_RELEASES_BUCKET      Default S3 bucket (default: releases.plow.co)
    26	  PLOW_RELEASES_PROFILE     Default AWS profile (default: plow)
    27	  PLOW_SPARKLE_ACCOUNT      Default Sparkle key account (default: plow-sparkle)
    28	  PLOW_KEEP_SIGNED_APP      When set to 1, keep a copy of the signed app at .build/Plow-signed.app
    29	EOF
    30	}
    31	
    32	repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"

   102	resolve_path() {
   103	  local path="$1"
   104	  if [[ "${path}" = /* ]]; then
   105	    echo "${path}"
   106	  else
   107	    echo "${repo_root}/${path}"
   108	  fi
   109	}
   110	
   111	plist_read() {
   112	    local plist_path="$1"
   113	    local key="$2"
   114	    /usr/bin/python3 -c "
   115	import plistlib, sys
   116	try:
   117	    with open(sys.argv[1], 'rb') as f:
   118	        d = plistlib.load(f)
   119	    print(d.get(sys.argv[2], ''), end='')
   120	except Exception:
   121	    pass
   122	" "${plist_path}" "${key}" 2>/dev/null || true
   123	}
   124	
   125	ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume() {
   126	  local mounted_plow_volumes
   127	  mounted_plow_volumes="$(
   128	    hdiutil info 2>/dev/null \
   129	      | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true
   130	  )"
   131	  mounted_plow_volumes="$(
   132	    printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" \
   133	      | sort -u
   134	  )"
   135	  [[ -z "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]] && return
   136	
   137	  echo "error: a Plow disk image is already mounted; eject it before packaging:" >&2
   138	  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
   139	  exit 1
   140	}

   142	app_bundle="$(resolve_path "${app_bundle}")"
   143	output="$(resolve_path "${output}")"
   144	entitlements="$(resolve_path "${entitlements}")"
   145	limactl_entitlements="$(resolve_path "${limactl_entitlements}")"
   146	
   147	if [[ -z "${identity}" ]]; then
   148	  [[ -n "${team_id}" ]] || { echo "error: PLOW_APPLE_TEAM_ID is required when --identity is not provided" >&2; exit 1; }
   149	  identity="$(security find-identity -v -p codesigning 2>/dev/null | sed -n "s/.*\"\\(Developer ID Application:.*(${team_id})\\)\"/\\1/p" | head -n 1)"
   150	fi
   151	
   152	[[ -n "${identity}" ]] || { echo "error: no Developer ID Application identity found for team ${team_id}; install one for that team before running release" >&2; exit 1; }
   153	if [[ -n "${team_id}" && "${identity}" != *"(${team_id})"* ]]; then
   154	  echo "error: selected signing identity does not match required Apple team ${team_id}: ${identity}" >&2
   155	  exit 1
   156	fi
   157	[[ -d "${app_bundle}" ]] || { echo "error: app bundle not found: ${app_bundle}" >&2; exit 1; }
   158	[[ -f "${entitlements}" ]] || { echo "error: entitlements file not found: ${entitlements}" >&2; exit 1; }
   159	[[ -f "${limactl_entitlements}" ]] || { echo "error: limactl entitlements file not found: ${limactl_entitlements}" >&2; exit 1; }
   160	[[ -x "${validate_script}" ]] || { echo "error: package validator not found: ${validate_script}" >&2; exit 1; }
   161	[[ -x "${stage_sparkle_script}" ]] || { echo "error: Sparkle stage script not found: ${stage_sparkle_script}" >&2; exit 1; }
   162	[[ -x "${publish_sparkle_script}" ]] || { echo "error: Sparkle publish script not found: ${publish_sparkle_script}" >&2; exit 1; }
   163	[[ -f "${dmg_ds_store}" ]] || { echo "error: DMG Finder metadata not found: ${dmg_ds_store}" >&2; exit 1; }
   164	[[ -f "${dmg_background}" ]] || { echo "error: DMG background not found: ${dmg_background}" >&2; exit 1; }
   165	
   166	echo "validating packaged app bundle..."
   167	"${validate_script}" --app-bundle "${app_bundle}"
   168	
   169	version="$(plist_read "${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" CFBundleShortVersionString)"
   170	build_number="$(plist_read "${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" CFBundleVersion)"
   171	sparkle_feed_url="$(plist_read "${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" SUFeedURL)"
   172	sparkle_public_key="$(plist_read "${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" SUPublicEDKey)"
   173	
   174	[[ -n "${version}" ]] || { echo "error: missing CFBundleShortVersionString in ${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" >&2; exit 1; }
   175	[[ -n "${build_number}" ]] || { echo "error: missing CFBundleVersion in ${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" >&2; exit 1; }
   176	[[ -n "${sparkle_feed_url}" ]] || { echo "error: missing SUFeedURL in ${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" >&2; exit 1; }
   177	[[ -n "${sparkle_public_key}" ]] || { echo "error: missing SUPublicEDKey in ${app_bundle}/Contents/Info.plist" >&2; exit 1; }
   178	
   179	release_prefix="${release_prefix#/}"
   180	release_prefix="${release_prefix%/}"
   181	prefix_with_slash=""
   182	if [[ -n "${release_prefix}" ]]; then
   183	  prefix_with_slash="${release_prefix}/"
   184	fi
   185	dmg_key="${prefix_with_slash}downloads/Plow-${version}-${build_number}.dmg"
   186	dmg_sha_key="${dmg_key}.sha256"
   187	sparkle_appcast_key="${prefix_with_slash}appcasts/Plow-${version}-${build_number}.xml"
   188	sparkle_archive_prefix="${prefix_with_slash}updates"
   189	sparkle_download_url_prefix="https://s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/${s3_bucket}/${sparkle_archive_prefix}"
   190	
   191	echo "using signing identity: ${identity}"
   192	echo "preferred Apple team id: ${team_id}"
   193	echo "using notary profile: ${notary_profile}"
   194

   196	  command -v "${cmd}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || { echo "error: required command not found: ${cmd}" >&2; exit 1; }
   197	done

   201	stage_dir="$(mktemp -d /tmp/phoenix-signed-beta.XXXXXX)"

   203	sparkle_stage_dir="$(mktemp -d /tmp/phoenix-sparkle-feed.XXXXXX)"
   204	mounted_volume=""
   205	
   206	cleanup() {
   207	  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
   208	    hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
   209	  fi
   210	  rm -rf "${stage_dir}"
   211	  rm -rf "${sparkle_stage_dir}"
   212	}
   213	trap cleanup EXIT
   214	
   215	mkdir -p "$(dirname "${output}")"
   216	ditto "${app_bundle}" "${stage_app}"
   217	ditto "${dmg_ds_store}" "${stage_dir}/.DS_Store"

   220	ln -s /Applications "${stage_dir}/Applications"
   221	xattr -cr "${stage_app}"

   223	while IFS= read -r -d '' file_path; do
   224	  file_desc="$(file -b "${file_path}" 2>/dev/null || true)"
   225	  if [[ "${file_desc}" == *"Mach-O"* ]]; then
   226	    sign_args=(--force --sign "${identity}" --timestamp)
   227	    if [[ "${file_desc}" == *"executable"* ]]; then
   228	      sign_args+=(--options runtime)
   229	    fi

   234	  fi

   284	submit_id="$(python3 -c 'import json,sys; print(json.load(sys.stdin).get("id",""))' <<<"${submit_output}")"
   285	submit_status="$(python3 -c 'import json,sys; print(json.load(sys.stdin).get("status",""))' <<<"${submit_output}")"

   291	  fi

     1	#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2	#
     3	# Interactively record the Finder window layout for the release DMG.
     4	#
     5	# Why this script exists
     6	# ----------------------
     7	# When the user double-clicks the released .dmg, Finder opens the volume
     8	# in a window with a custom background image, hidden toolbar/sidebar,
     9	# and Plow.app + Applications icons in fixed positions. None of that
    10	# styling can be set programmatically by hdiutil — Finder reads it from
    11	# a .DS_Store at the volume root. We used to set up that .DS_Store with
    12	# AppleScript at packaging time, but that automation was flaky in CI and
    13	# was removed in favor of shipping a pre-recorded .DS_Store checked in
    14	# at app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store. plowd-beta-package-signed ditto's that
    15	# file into the staging dir before hdiutil create. So: edits to the
    16	# install-window appearance must be made by re-running this script and
    17	# committing the resulting .DS_Store.
    18	#
    19	# How it works
    20	# ------------
    21	# 1. Stage the same files plowd-beta-package-signed ships: Plow.app,
    22	#    Applications symlink, .background/background.tiff.
    23	# 2. Create a writable (UDRW) DMG and mount it. Finder pops open the
    24	#    volume window; the user arranges it (View Options for background,
    25	#    icon size, arrangement; drag for icon positions and window size).
    26	# 3. User closes the window (Cmd-W), which prompts Finder to flush
    27	#    .DS_Store, and presses Enter at the script's prompt.
    28	# 4. Eject and re-mount. The eject is what guarantees Finder has
    29	#    written .DS_Store to disk; reading it from a still-mounted volume
    30	#    can return a stale or empty file.
    31	# 5. Copy /Volumes/Plow/.DS_Store -> app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store and
    32	#    detach.
    33	#
    34	# Display-size caveat
    35	# -------------------
    36	# .DS_Store stores the install window's bounds as absolute screen
    37	# coordinates relative to the main display. If you record on a large
    38	# display with the window at (e.g.) 2000,1500, Finder on a small
    39	# laptop will reposition the off-screen window to fit, which loses
    40	# your placement. Record near the top-left of your screen and keep the
    41	# window modest (~680x420 fits every Mac display).
    42	#
    43	# Verifying after recording
    44	# -------------------------
    45	# Before committing, build a release DMG (or stage by hand and run
    46	# hdiutil create -format ULFO with the new .DS_Store ditto'd in) and
    47	# open it to confirm Finder honors the layout. The captured .DS_Store
    48	# should grow noticeably (~6 KB+) when a background picture is set;
    49	# a near-8 KB unchanged size suggests the picture didn't take.
    50	#
    51	# Why a separate script (vs inline in plowd-beta-package-signed)
    52	# --------------------------------------------------------------
    53	# This is a one-off authoring tool with mandatory human-in-Finder
    54	# steps; the release script is unattended CI. Keeping them separate
    55	# makes the release path deterministic (just `ditto` a checked-in
    56	# blob) and lets layout changes go through a normal code review of
    57	# the .DS_Store diff.
    58	set -euo pipefail
    59	
    60	usage() {
    61	  cat <<'EOF'
    62	Usage: plowd-record-dmg-layout [--app <path>]
    63	
    64	Records app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store from an interactive Finder layout
    65	session. Mounts a writable scratch DMG that mirrors the staging
    66	plowd-beta-package-signed ships, drops you into Finder to arrange the
    67	install window, then captures the resulting .DS_Store back into the
    68	repo when you press Enter at the prompt.
    69	
    70	Workflow once mounted at /Volumes/Plow:
    71	  1. View > as Icons (Cmd-1)
    72	  2. View > Hide Toolbar (Opt-Cmd-T)
    73	  3. View > Show View Options (Cmd-J)
    74	       - size/position the window (keep it under ~680x420 and near
    75	         the top-left of your screen so it fits on small displays)
    76	       - drag .background/background.tiff into Background > Picture
    77	         (open a second Finder window, Cmd-Shift-. to show hidden
    78	         files, then drag the .tiff into the well; the file picker
    79	         is unreliable for hidden paths)
    80	       - icon size, text size, arrangement = None
    81	  4. Drag Plow.app and Applications icons into position
    82	  5. Close the volume window (Cmd-W) to flush .DS_Store
    83	  6. Press Enter at this script's prompt to capture
    84	
    85	Options:
    86	  --app <path>   Path to the .app to stage. Defaults to the release
    87	                 build at .build/xcode-derived/Build/Products/Release/
    88	                 Plow.app, falling back to /Applications/Plow.app
    89	                 (which is fine for layout-only iteration since icon
    90	                 positions are recorded by filename).
    91	  -h, --help     Show this message.
    92	EOF
    93	}
    94	
    95	repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"
    96	app_path=""
    97	
    98	while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
    99	  case "$1" in
   100	    --app)
   101	      app_path="${2:-}"
   102	      shift 2
   103	      ;;
   104	    -h|--help)
   105	      usage
   106	      exit 0
   107	      ;;
   108	    *)
   109	      echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
   110	      usage >&2
   111	      exit 1
   112	      ;;
   113	  esac
   114	done
   115	
   116	if [[ -z "${app_path}" ]]; then
   117	  release_app="${repo_root}/.build/xcode-derived/Build/Products/Release/Plow.app"
   118	  if [[ -d "${release_app}" ]]; then
   119	    app_path="${release_app}"
   120	  elif [[ -d "/Applications/Plow.app" ]]; then
   121	    app_path="/Applications/Plow.app"
   122	    echo "note: using /Applications/Plow.app (no release build found)"
   123	  else
   124	    echo "error: no Plow.app found; pass --app <path>, run 'just app release', or install via /plow-prod-install" >&2
   125	    exit 1
   126	  fi
   127	fi
   128	[[ -d "${app_path}" ]] || { echo "error: Plow.app not found at ${app_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
   129	
   130	bg_src="${repo_root}/app/plowd/dmg/background.tiff"
   131	ds_dest="${repo_root}/app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store"
   132	[[ -f "${bg_src}" ]] || { echo "error: background not found: ${bg_src}" >&2; exit 1; }
   133	
   134	mounted_plow_volumes="$(hdiutil info 2>/dev/null | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true)"
   135	mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"
   136	if [[ -n "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]]; then
   137	  echo "error: a Plow volume is already mounted; eject it before recording:" >&2
   138	  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
   139	  exit 1
   140	fi
   141	
   142	work_dir="$(mktemp -d /tmp/plowd-dmg-record.XXXXXX)"
   143	stage_dir="${work_dir}/stage"
   144	rw_dmg="${work_dir}/layout.dmg"
   145	mounted_volume=""
   146	cleanup() {
   147	  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
   148	    hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
   149	  fi
   150	  rm -rf "${work_dir}"
   151	}
   152	trap cleanup EXIT
   153	
   154	mkdir -p "${stage_dir}/.background"
   155	ditto "${app_path}" "${stage_dir}/Plow.app"
   156	ditto "${bg_src}" "${stage_dir}/.background/background.tiff"
   157	ln -s /Applications "${stage_dir}/Applications"
   158	
   159	hdiutil create -volname "Plow" -srcfolder "${stage_dir}" -ov -format UDRW "${rw_dmg}" >/dev/null
   160	attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${rw_dmg}" -readwrite -noverify)"
   161	mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | sed -n 's|.*\(/Volumes/.*\)$|\1|p' | head -n 1)"
   162	[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to determine mounted volume for ${rw_dmg}" >&2; exit 1; }
   163	
   164	cat <<EOF
   165	
   166	mounted at ${mounted_volume}
   167	
   168	In Finder:
   169	  - View > as Icons (Cmd-1)
   170	  - View > Hide Toolbar (Opt-Cmd-T)
   171	  - View > Show View Options (Cmd-J)
   172	      * size/position the window
   173	      * drag .background/background.tiff into Background > Picture
   174	        (Cmd-Shift-. in the picker shows hidden files)
   175	      * set icon size, text size, arrangement = None
   176	  - position Plow.app and Applications icons
   177	  - close the window (Cmd-W) to flush .DS_Store
   178	
   179	EOF
   180	printf "Press Enter when done... "
   181	read -r _ </dev/tty
   182	
   183	hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null
   184	mounted_volume=""
   185	
   186	attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${rw_dmg}" -readwrite -noverify -noautoopen)"
   187	mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | sed -n 's|.*\(/Volumes/.*\)$|\1|p' | head -n 1)"
   188	[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to remount ${rw_dmg}" >&2; exit 1; }

   191	  echo "error: no .DS_Store in mounted volume — did Finder finalize the layout (Cmd-W)?" >&2
   192	  exit 1
   193	}

   197	mounted_volume=""

     1	#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2	# Mount a Plow DMG and assert it has no custom volume icon (PLO-29 regression
     3	# guard) and that the volume name is "Plow". Detaches before exiting.
     4	set -euo pipefail
     5	
     6	usage() {
     7	  cat <<'EOF'
     8	Usage: plowd-verify-dmg [<dmg-path>]
     9	
    10	Mounts the given DMG, asserts the mounted volume is named "Plow" and has no
    11	.VolumeIcon.icns at its root, then detaches. With no argument, defaults to
    12	.build/Plow.dmg relative to the repo root. A relative argument is resolved
    13	against the repo root.
    14	EOF
    15	}
    16	
    17	repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"
    18	default_dmg=".build/Plow.dmg"
    19	
    20	dmg_path=""
    21	case "${1:-}" in
    22	  -h|--help)
    23	    usage
    24	    exit 0
    25	    ;;
    26	  "")
    27	    dmg_path="${repo_root}/${default_dmg}"
    28	    ;;
    29	  -*)
    30	    echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
    31	    usage >&2
    32	    exit 1
    33	    ;;
    34	  *)
    35	    dmg_path="$1"
    36	    if (( $# > 1 )); then
    37	      echo "error: unexpected extra arguments: ${*:2}" >&2
    38	      usage >&2
    39	      exit 1
    40	    fi
    41	    ;;
    42	esac
    43	
    44	if [[ "${dmg_path}" != /* ]]; then
    45	  dmg_path="${repo_root}/${dmg_path}"
    46	fi
    47	
    48	[[ -f "${dmg_path}" ]] || { echo "error: DMG not found: ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
    49	
    50	# Refuse to run when a Plow volume is already mounted: the new mountpoint
    51	# would be "Plow 1" / "Plow 2" / ..., which would mask a real regression in
    52	# the volume-name assertion below.
    53	mounted_plow_volumes="$(hdiutil info 2>/dev/null | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true)"
    54	mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"
    55	if [[ -n "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]]; then
    56	  echo "error: a Plow volume is already mounted; eject it before verifying:" >&2
    57	  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
    58	  exit 1
    59	fi
    60	
    61	mounted_volume=""
    62	cleanup() {
    63	  local rc=$?
    64	  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
    65	    if [[ "${rc}" -eq 0 ]]; then
    66	      # Success path: detach failure (e.g. volume busy) must be fatal.
    67	      # Otherwise the next release retry trips ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume
    68	      # in plowd-beta-package-signed and aborts on a leaked mount.
    69	      if ! hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}"; then
    70	        echo "error: failed to detach ${mounted_volume} after successful verify" >&2
    71	        exit 1
    72	      fi
    73	    else
    74	      # Failure path: don't let detach noise mask the real error.
    75	      hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
    76	    fi
    77	  fi
    78	  exit "${rc}"
    79	}
    80	trap cleanup EXIT
    81	
    82	attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${dmg_path}" -nobrowse -readonly)"
    83	# Real `hdiutil attach` prints one line per partition; the data partition's
    84	# last whitespace-delimited field is the mount point. Other lines (e.g. the
    85	# GUID partition scheme) end in a partition-type token that doesn't start
    86	# with "/". Pick the last line whose final field is an absolute path —
    87	# works for both real hdiutil's multi-line tabular output and a single-line
    88	# stub.
    89	mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | awk '$NF ~ /^\// { last=$NF } END { print last }')"
    90	[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to mount ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
    91	
    92	volume_name="$(basename "${mounted_volume}")"
    93	[[ "${volume_name}" == "Plow" ]] || { echo "error: mounted volume name is '${volume_name}', expected 'Plow'" >&2; exit 1; }
    94	
    95	[[ ! -e "${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns" ]] || {
    96	  echo "error: ${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns exists; PLO-29 regression: DMG ships a custom volume icon" >&2
    97	  exit 1
    98	}
    99	
   100	echo "ok: ${dmg_path} mounts as 'Plow' with no custom volume icon"

   234	              cat >/dev/null
   235	              printf 'Loaded image: plow-demo/openclaw-latest:2026.4.26\\n'
   236	              printf 'Loaded image: plow-demo/openclaw-latest:latest\\n'
   237	            fi
   238	            """
   239	        ),
   240	        encoding="utf-8",
   241	    )
   242	    (fake_bin / "nerdctl").chmod(0o755)
   243	
   244	    result = _run_provision(tmp_path, fake_bin)
   245	    assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
   246	    importer = tmp_path / "libexec" / "import-runtime-images.sh"
   247	
   248	    image_tar = tmp_path / "plow-starter.tar.zst"
   249	    image_tar.write_text("runtime image bytes\n", encoding="utf-8")
   250	    image_sha = hashlib.sha256(image_tar.read_bytes()).hexdigest()
   251	    env_file = tmp_path / "runtime.env"
   252	    env_file.write_text(
   253	        textwrap.dedent(
   254	            f"""
   255	            RUNTIME_KEY=plow-starter
   256	            IMAGE_TAR={image_tar}
   257	            IMAGE_SHA256={image_sha}
   258	            """
   259	        ).strip()
   260	        + "\n",
   261	        encoding="utf-8",
   262	    )
   263	    stamp_dir = tmp_path / "stamps"
   264	
   265	    first = subprocess.run(
   266	        ["bash", str(importer)],
   267	        capture_output=True,
   268	        text=True,
   269	        env={
   270	            **subprocess.os.environ,
   271	            "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
   272	            "PLOW_RUNTIME_ENV_FILE": str(env_file),
   273	            "PLOW_RUNTIME_IMAGE_STAMP_DIR": str(stamp_dir),
   274	        },
   275	    )
   276	    assert first.returncode == 0, first.stderr
   277	
   278	    second = subprocess.run(
   279	        ["bash", str(importer)],
   280	        capture_output=True,
   281	        text=True,
   282	        env={
   283	            **subprocess.os.environ,
   284	            "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
   285	            "PLOW_RUNTIME_ENV_FILE": str(env_file),
   286	            "PLOW_RUNTIME_IMAGE_STAMP_DIR": str(stamp_dir),
   287	        },
   288	    )
   289	    assert second.returncode == 0, second.stderr
   290	    assert "already loaded, skipping" in second.stderr
   291	
   292	    assert (stamp_dir / f"{image_sha}.loaded").read_text(encoding="utf-8") == (
   293	        f"plow/plow-starter:{image_sha[:12]}\n"
   294	    )
   295	    nerdctl_calls = nerdctl_log.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines()
   296	    assert nerdctl_calls == [
   297	        "load",
   298	        f"tag plow-demo/openclaw-latest:2026.4.26 plow/plow-starter:{image_sha[:12]}",
   299	        "rmi plow-demo/openclaw-latest:2026.4.26",
   300	        "rmi plow-demo/openclaw-latest:latest",
   301	    ]

   337	def test_git_ref_script_defaults_to_parent_commit_for_stable_rebuilds(tmp_path):
   338	    repo_root = tmp_path / "repo"
   339	    repo_root.mkdir()
   340	
   341	    def git(*args: str) -> str:
   342	        result = subprocess.run(
   343	            ["git", *args],
   344	            capture_output=True,
   345	            text=True,
   346	            cwd=repo_root,
   347	            check=True,
   348	        )
   349	        return result.stdout.strip()
   350	
   351	    git("init")
   352	    git("config", "user.name", "Test User")
   353	    git("config", "user.email", "test@example.com")
   354	
   355	    tracked_file = repo_root / "tracked.txt"
   356	    tracked_file.write_text("first\n", encoding="utf-8")
   357	    git("add", "tracked.txt")
   358	    git("commit", "-m", "first")
   359	    parent_ref = git("rev-parse", "--short=7", "HEAD")
   360	
   361	    tracked_file.write_text("second\n", encoding="utf-8")
   362	    git("commit", "-am", "second")
   363	
   364	    result = subprocess.run(
   365	        [
   366	            "bash",
   367	            "-lc",
   368	            'source "$1"; REPO_ROOT="$2"; compute_git_ref',
   369	            "bash",
   370	            str(GIT_REF_SCRIPT),
   371	            str(repo_root),
   372	        ],
   373	        capture_output=True,
   374	        text=True,
   375	        cwd=REPO_ROOT,
   376	    )
   377	
   378	    assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
   379	    assert result.stdout.strip() == parent_ref

   382	def test_signed_package_script_stages_release_dmg_contents(tmp_path):
   383	    app_bundle = tmp_path / "Plow.app"
   384	    output = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
   385	    fake_log_dir = tmp_path / "fake-logs"
   386	    fake_log_dir.mkdir()
   387	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "fake-bin"
   388	    fake_bin.mkdir()
   389	    _create_minimal_valid_app_bundle(app_bundle)
   390	    _write_fake_release_commands(fake_bin)
   391	
   392	    env = {
   393	        **subprocess.os.environ,
   394	        "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
   395	        "FAKE_LOG_DIR": str(fake_log_dir),
   396	        "PLOW_RUNTIME_UPLOAD_SCRIPT": str(fake_bin / "upload-runtime-artifacts.sh"),
   397	        "SPARKLE_BIN_DIR": str(fake_bin),
   398	    }
   399	
   400	    result = subprocess.run(
   401	        [
   402	            str(SIGNED_PACKAGE_SCRIPT),
   403	            "--app-bundle",
   404	            str(app_bundle),
   405	            "--output",
   406	            str(output),
   407	            "--identity",
   408	            "Developer ID Application: Example (3559PD337Z)",
   409	            "--notary-profile",
   410	            "test-notary",
   411	            "--s3-bucket",
   412	            "test-bucket",
   413	            "--release-prefix",
   414	            "beta",
   415	            "--s3-profile",
   416	            "test-profile",
   417	        ],
   418	        capture_output=True,
   419	        text=True,
   420	        cwd=REPO_ROOT,
   421	        env=env,
   422	    )
   423	
   424	    assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
   425	    assert output.exists()
   426	
   427	    hdiutil_log = (fake_log_dir / "hdiutil.log").read_text()
   428	    assert "create" in hdiutil_log
   429	    assert "-format ULFO" in hdiutil_log
   430	    # PLO-29: DMG is created directly as ULFO; the old UDRW->convert dance
   431	    # only existed to host a kHasCustomIcon FinderInfo write on a mounted
   432	    # volume, which we no longer do.
   433	    assert "-format UDRW" not in hdiutil_log
   434	    assert "convert" not in hdiutil_log
   435	    # PLO-29: the post-staple verifier is mandatory — its banner appears in
   436	    # stdout and `hdiutil attach` of the final DMG appears in the hdiutil
   437	    # log. There is no test-only bypass.
   438	    assert "verifying final DMG against PLO-29 contract" in result.stdout
   439	    assert f"attach {output}" in hdiutil_log
   440	
   441	    staged_dir = fake_log_dir / "captured-srcfolder"
   442	    assert (staged_dir / "Plow.app").is_dir()
   443	    assert (staged_dir / "Applications").is_symlink()
   444	    # The DMG ships curated Finder window metadata (window position/size,
   445	    # icon layout, background association). This is distinct from
   446	    # .VolumeIcon.icns — .DS_Store affects the *open Finder window*,
   447	    # .VolumeIcon.icns would replace the *disk icon* (PLO-29 forbids).
   448	    assert (staged_dir / ".DS_Store").is_file()
   449	    assert (staged_dir / ".background" / "background.tiff").is_file()
   450	    # PLO-29: the mounted volume must show the default macOS volume icon,
   451	    # so the staged srcfolder must not ship a .VolumeIcon.icns.
   452	    assert not (staged_dir / ".VolumeIcon.icns").exists()
   453	    assert not (staged_dir / "Plow-rw.dmg").exists()
   454

   456	@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
   457	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_dmg_shipping_volume_icon(tmp_path):
   458	    """PLO-29 artifact-level guard. Catches the failure mode that
   459	    ``test_signed_package_script_stages_release_dmg_contents`` cannot:
   460	    a regression that re-attaches the DMG post-``hdiutil create``
   461	    and re-stages a custom volume icon at the final-image stage. We build
   462	    three real DMGs with hdiutil and assert plowd-verify-dmg accepts the
   463	    clean one and rejects each regression shape.
   464	
   465	    plowd-verify-dmg is wired into plowd-beta-package-signed between staple
   466	    and S3 upload, so a rejection here aborts ``just release`` before any
   467	    artifact ships."""
   468	    # Refuse to run if a real Plow volume is already mounted: the script
   469	    # bails on that and our assertions would tag the wrong failure mode.
   470	    info = subprocess.run(
   471	        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   472	    )
   473	    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
   474	        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
   475	
   476	    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
   477	    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
   478	    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
   479	
   480	    def make_dmg(dmg_path: Path, *, volname: str) -> None:
   481	        subprocess.run(
   482	            [
   483	                "hdiutil", "create",
   484	                "-volname", volname,
   485	                "-srcfolder", str(stage),
   486	                "-ov",
   487	                "-format", "ULFO",
   488	                str(dmg_path),
   489	            ],
   490	            check=True, capture_output=True,
   491	        )
   492	
   493	    def run_verify(dmg_path: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
   494	        return subprocess.run(
   495	            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), str(dmg_path)],
   496	            capture_output=True, text=True,
   497	        )
   498	
   499	    # Happy path: clean Plow DMG with no .VolumeIcon must pass.
   500	    clean_dmg = tmp_path / "clean.dmg"
   501	    make_dmg(clean_dmg, volname="Plow")
   502	    ok = run_verify(clean_dmg)
   503	    assert ok.returncode == 0, f"clean DMG rejected: stdout={ok.stdout!r} stderr={ok.stderr!r}"
   504	
   505	    # Regression #1: someone re-introduces .VolumeIcon.icns at the volume root.
   506	    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").write_text("fake-icns")
   507	    iconed_dmg = tmp_path / "iconed.dmg"
   508	    make_dmg(iconed_dmg, volname="Plow")
   509	    fail = run_verify(iconed_dmg)
   510	    assert fail.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG that ships .VolumeIcon.icns"
   511	    assert ".VolumeIcon.icns exists" in fail.stderr
   512	
   513	    # Regression #2: someone parameterizes -volname to something other than "Plow".
   514	    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").unlink()

   518	    assert fail2.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG with wrong volume name"
   519	    assert "expected 'Plow'" in fail2.stderr

   522	@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
   523	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_propagates_detach_failure_on_success_path(tmp_path):
   524	    """Round-2: if `hdiutil detach` fails on the success path (e.g. the
   525	    volume is busy), plowd-verify-dmg must exit non-zero. The previous
   526	    `|| true` swallowed the failure and returned 0, leaking /Volumes/Plow,
   527	    which then tripped ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume on the next release
   528	    retry. This test injects an `hdiutil` wrapper whose `detach` always
   529	    fails and asserts the script surfaces it."""
   530	    info = subprocess.run(
   531	        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   532	    )
   533	    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
   534	        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
   535	
   536	    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
   537	    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
   538	    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
   539	    dmg = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
   540	    subprocess.run(
   541	        [
   542	            "hdiutil", "create",
   543	            "-volname", "Plow",
   544	            "-srcfolder", str(stage),
   545	            "-ov",
   546	            "-format", "ULFO",
   547	            str(dmg),
   548	        ],
   549	        check=True, capture_output=True,
   550	    )
   551	
   552	    real_hdiutil = subprocess.run(
   553	        ["which", "hdiutil"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   554	    ).stdout.strip()
   555	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
   556	    fake_bin.mkdir()
   557	    wrapper = fake_bin / "hdiutil"
   558	    wrapper.write_text(
   559	        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\n"
   560	        f'if [[ "$1" == "detach" ]]; then\n'
   561	        f'  echo "fake: detach failure (test injection)" >&2\n'
   562	        f'  exit 16\n'
   563	        f'fi\n'
   564	        f'exec "{real_hdiutil}" "$@"\n'
   565	    )
   566	    wrapper.chmod(0o755)
   567	
   568	    try:
   569	        result = subprocess.run(
   570	            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), str(dmg)],
   571	            capture_output=True, text=True,
   572	            env={
   573	                **subprocess.os.environ,
   574	                "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
   575	            },
   576	        )
   577	        assert result.returncode != 0, (
   578	            f"verify-dmg returned 0 despite detach failure; mount leaked.\n"
   579	            f"stdout={result.stdout!r}\nstderr={result.stderr!r}"
   580	        )
   581	        assert "failed to detach" in result.stderr, (
   582	            f"expected 'failed to detach' in stderr, got: {result.stderr!r}"
   583	        )
   584	    finally:
   585	        # Real hdiutil to clean up the leaked mount the wrapper refused to release.
   586	        subprocess.run(
   587	            [real_hdiutil, "detach", "/Volumes/Plow"],
   588	            capture_output=True,
   589	        )
   590	
   591	
   592	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   593	# Cross-platform verifier tests. These drive plowd-verify-dmg through a fake
   594	# `hdiutil` that points the verifier at a tmp directory whose contents and
   595	# basename the test controls. They exercise the same accept/reject code path
   596	# the real release run takes — no env-skip, no green skip — so the verifier's
   597	# decision logic is covered on every CI lane (including non-macOS ones that
   598	# can't run real hdiutil at all).
   599	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   600	def _write_verifier_fake_hdiutil(fake_bin: Path, mount_path: Path) -> None:
   601	    """Stub `hdiutil` so plowd-verify-dmg attaches to ``mount_path``.
   602	
   603	    The verifier shells out to `hdiutil info` (mount listing), `hdiutil
   604	    attach` (which prints a tabular line whose final column is the mount
   605	    point) and `hdiutil detach` on cleanup. The stub:
   606	
   607	    - prints nothing for `info` (no /Volumes/Plow already mounted)
   608	    - prints `/dev/disk9s1 Apple_APFS <mount_path>` for `attach`
   609	    - succeeds for `detach`
   610	
   611	    The test pre-stages ``mount_path`` with whatever contents and basename
   612	    it wants the verifier to see.
   613	    """
   614	    fake_bin.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
   615	    hdiutil = fake_bin / "hdiutil"
   616	    hdiutil.write_text(
   617	        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\n"
   618	        "case \"$1\" in\n"
   619	        "  info) exit 0 ;;\n"
   620	        f"  attach) printf '/dev/disk9s1 Apple_APFS %s\\n' '{mount_path}'; exit 0 ;;\n"
   621	        "  detach) exit 0 ;;\n"
   622	        "  *) exit 1 ;;\n"
   623	        "esac\n"
   624	    )
   625	    hdiutil.chmod(0o755)
   626	
   627	
   628	def _run_verifier_with_fake_hdiutil(
   629	    tmp_path: Path,
   630	    *,
   631	    mount_basename: str,
   632	    stage_volume_icon: bool,
   633	) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
   634	    """Stage a fake mount + DMG file, run plowd-verify-dmg, return result."""
   635	    mount_path = tmp_path / "fake-mount" / mount_basename
   636	    mount_path.mkdir(parents=True)
   637	    if stage_volume_icon:
   638	        (mount_path / ".VolumeIcon.icns").write_bytes(b"fake-icns")
   639	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"

   692	def test_just_dmg_verify_recipe_is_thin_alias_to_verifier(tmp_path):
   693	    """`just app dmg-verify` is the public no-arg entrypoint; it must be a
   694	    pass-through to plowd-verify-dmg, with no extra flags or wrapping that
   695	    would land it on a different code path than the inline release-script
   696	    call. We assert the recipe body forwards positional args verbatim and
   697	    does not pin a flag like `--dmg`."""
   698	    just_text = (REPO_ROOT / "app" / "justfile").read_text()
   699	    # Pull out the dmg-verify recipe block (header line + indented body).
   700	    match = re.search(
   701	        r"^dmg-verify[^\n]*:\n((?:    [^\n]*\n)+)",
   702	        just_text,
   703	        re.MULTILINE,
   704	    )
   705	    assert match is not None, "dmg-verify recipe not found in app/justfile"
   706	    body = match.group(1)
   707	    assert "plowd-verify-dmg" in body
   708	    # Round-3 collapse: the recipe must not pin --dmg or any other flag —
   709	    # one positional pass-through, same code path as the inline release-
   710	    # script call.
   711	    assert "--dmg" not in body, (
   712	        f"dmg-verify recipe still passes --dmg; should be a positional "
   713	        f"pass-through. Recipe body:\n{body}"
   714	    )

   951	def _create_minimal_valid_app_bundle(app_bundle: Path) -> None:
   952	    contents_root = app_bundle / "Contents"
