  1033	def test_validate_package_rejects_bundle_missing_plowd_dist_info(tmp_path):
  1034	    """A packaged runtime that exists structurally but lacks plowd-*.dist-info/
  1035	    is the exact regression #478 shape: site-packages/ is present, all files
  1036	    pass the existence check, but plowd dies at import with PackageNotFoundError
  1037	    because importlib.metadata can't find the metadata."""
  1038	    app_bundle = tmp_path / "Plow.app"
  1039	    _create_minimal_valid_app_bundle(app_bundle)
  1040	
  1041	    # Sanity: the unmodified bundle passes validation.
  1042	    ok = subprocess.run(
  1043	        [str(VALIDATE_PACKAGE_SCRIPT), "--app-bundle", str(app_bundle), "--mode", "offline"],
  1044	        capture_output=True,
  1045	        text=True,
  1046	    )
  1047	    assert ok.returncode == 0, f"baseline bundle should validate cleanly, got: {ok.stderr}"
  1048	
  1049	    # Remove the dist-info; site-packages/ itself stays so this isn't caught
  1050	    # by the existing required_runtime_paths loop.
  1051	    dist_info = (
  1052	        app_bundle / "Contents" / "Resources" / "runtime"
  1053	        / "site-packages" / "plowd-0.1.1.dist-info"
  1054	    )
  1055	    import shutil
  1056	    shutil.rmtree(dist_info)
  1057	
  1058	    fail = subprocess.run(
  1059	        [str(VALIDATE_PACKAGE_SCRIPT), "--app-bundle", str(app_bundle), "--mode", "offline"],
  1060	        capture_output=True,
  1061	        text=True,
  1062	    )
  1063	    assert fail.returncode != 0, "validate-package must reject a bundle missing plowd dist-info"
  1064	    assert "plowd-*.dist-info" in fail.stderr, (
  1065	        f"error message should mention the missing dist-info; got stderr:\n{fail.stderr}"
  1066	    )

  1079	def test_stage_runtime_installs_plowd_dist_info():
  1080	    """plowd's `importlib.metadata.version("plowd")` calls need `plowd-*.dist-info/`
  1081	    on sys.path. The rsync of the source tree into `${stage_dir}/plowd` doesn't
  1082	    include metadata, so plowd-stage-runtime must explicitly install plowd into
  1083	    site-packages alongside the external deps so the dist-info is present.
  1084	    Without this, packaged apps die at import with PackageNotFoundError before
  1085	    binding the HTTP port (regression #478)."""
  1086	    stage_script = (
  1087	        REPO_ROOT / "app" / "plowd" / "scripts" / "plowd-stage-runtime"
  1088	    ).read_text(encoding="utf-8")
  1089	
  1090	    # Whitespace-tolerant: pin the unique combination of flags that identifies
  1091	    # the dist-info install (--no-deps + ${project_root}) without locking the
  1092	    # script to a specific line-continuation/indent style.
  1093	    assert re.search(
  1094	        r'uv pip install\b[^\n]*'
  1095	        r'(?:\\\s*\n[^\n]*)*'
  1096	        r'--target\s+"\$\{stage_dir\}/site-packages"'
  1097	        r'[^\n]*(?:\\\s*\n[^\n]*)*'
  1098	        r'--no-deps'
  1099	        r'[^\n]*(?:\\\s*\n[^\n]*)*'
  1100	        r'"\$\{project_root\}"',
  1101	        stage_script,
  1102	    ), (
  1103	        "plowd-stage-runtime must `uv pip install --no-deps` plowd into "
  1104	        "${stage_dir}/site-packages so the daemon's importlib.metadata.version"
  1105	        "('plowd') call resolves"
  1106	    )

  1228	def test_release_build_recipe_honors_caller_supplied_signing_identity():
  1229	    """Pin the PLOW_CODE_SIGN_IDENTITY contract introduced in PR #521.
  1230	
  1231	    The Release build path must:
  1232	      1. Default to ad-hoc *only when* the caller hasn't set
  1233	         PLOW_CODE_SIGN_IDENTITY — otherwise the install skills can't
  1234	         opt into a real Developer ID cert.
  1235	      2. Re-sign post-packaging using whatever identity is set, not a
  1236	         hardcoded `-`. plowd-package-runtime rsyncs into
  1237	         Contents/Resources after Xcode signs; without the re-sign,
  1238	         team-signed bundles ship with an invalid seal.
  1239	    """
  1240	    app_justfile = (REPO_ROOT / "app" / "justfile").read_text(encoding="utf-8")
  1241	
  1242	    assert (
  1243	        'if [[ "$configuration" == "Release" && -z "${PLOW_CODE_SIGN_IDENTITY:-}" ]]; then'
  1244	        in app_justfile
  1245	    ), "Release default must guard PLOW_CODE_SIGN_IDENTITY rather than clobber it"
  1246	    assert 'export PLOW_CODE_SIGN_IDENTITY="-"' in app_justfile
  1247	
  1248	    assert (
  1249	        'if [[ "$configuration" == "Release" && -n "${PLOW_CODE_SIGN_IDENTITY:-}" ]]; then'
  1250	        in app_justfile
  1251	    ), "post-package re-sign must guard on identity set, not on hardcoded `-`"
  1252	    assert (
  1253	        'codesign --force --sign "${PLOW_CODE_SIGN_IDENTITY}" --deep --entitlements'
  1254	        in app_justfile
  1255	    ), "post-package re-sign must honor any PLOW_CODE_SIGN_IDENTITY, not a hardcoded `-`"

330-3893:+# Mounts a writable scratch DMG with production staging, drops you into
331:3894:+# Finder to arrange it, then captures the resulting .DS_Store into
332:3895:+# app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store. That checked-in .DS_Store is shipped verbatim
333:3896:+# by plowd-beta-package-signed in CI; without re-running this recipe,
334-3897:+# layout changes won't reach users. Use whenever you change
335-3898:+# background.tiff, want to move icons, or need to resize the install
336-3899:+# window.
337-3900:+#
338-3901:+# Workflow: arrange the Finder window, close it with Cmd-W (flushes
339:3902:+# .DS_Store), then press Enter at the script's prompt. Defaults --app
340-3903:+# to the release build, falling back to /Applications/Plow.app. See
341:3904:+# plowd/scripts/plowd-record-dmg-layout for shortcuts and caveats.
342-3905:+#
343-3906:+# Re-record the Finder window layout used by the release DMG.

360:4008:+++ b/app/plowd/scripts/plowd-record-dmg-layout
361-4010:+#!/usr/bin/env bash
362-4011:+#
363-4012:+# Interactively record the Finder window layout for the release DMG.
--
368-4017:+# in a window with a custom background image, hidden toolbar/sidebar,
369-4018:+# and Plow.app + Applications icons in fixed positions. None of that
370-4019:+# styling can be set programmatically by hdiutil — Finder reads it from
371:4020:+# a .DS_Store at the volume root. We used to set up that .DS_Store with
372-4021:+# AppleScript at packaging time, but that automation was flaky in CI and
373:4022:+# was removed in favor of shipping a pre-recorded .DS_Store checked in
374:4023:+# at app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store. plowd-beta-package-signed ditto's that
375-4024:+# file into the staging dir before hdiutil create. So: edits to the
376-4025:+# install-window appearance must be made by re-running this script and
377:4026:+# committing the resulting .DS_Store.
378-4027:+#
379-4028:+# How it works
380-4029:+# ------------
381:4030:+# 1. Stage the same files plowd-beta-package-signed ships: Plow.app,
382-4031:+#    Applications symlink, .background/background.tiff.
383-4032:+# 2. Create a writable (UDRW) DMG and mount it. Finder pops open the
384-4033:+#    volume window; the user arranges it (View Options for background,
385-4034:+#    icon size, arrangement; drag for icon positions and window size).
386-4035:+# 3. User closes the window (Cmd-W), which prompts Finder to flush
387:4036:+#    .DS_Store, and presses Enter at the script's prompt.
388-4037:+# 4. Eject and re-mount. The eject is what guarantees Finder has
389:4038:+#    written .DS_Store to disk; reading it from a still-mounted volume
390-4039:+#    can return a stale or empty file.
391:4040:+# 5. Copy /Volumes/Plow/.DS_Store -> app/plowd/dmg/.DS_Store and
392-4041:+#    detach.
393-4042:+#
394-4043:+# Display-size caveat
395-4044:+# -------------------

## [performance] findings

### Surveyed
- Direct ULFO DMG creation in `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-beta-package-signed:263` — clean; removes the older writable-DMG/convert pass, so release I/O goes down overall.
- Mandatory final artifact verification in `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-beta-package-signed:301` — clean; one extra `hdiutil attach`/detach on a release-only path before upload.
- `plowd-verify-dmg` mount detection and checks in `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-verify-dmg:53` and `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-verify-dmg:82` — clean; bounded by mounted volume count and a single DMG mount.
- macOS CI plowd test wiring in `.github/workflows/test.yml:31` — clean for this PR; it duplicates the daemon suite on macOS, but that is CI-only and not a current timeout/OOM risk from the diff.
- Real-`hdiutil` regression tests in `app/plowd/tests/test_release_scripts.py:456` and `app/plowd/tests/test_release_scripts.py:522` — clean; they create a handful of tiny DMGs and do not scale with user data.
- Interactive layout recorder in `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-record-dmg-layout:154` — clean; expensive app copy and writable DMG creation are manual authoring steps, not request/release hot paths.
